### [189] [Hybrid Classical-Quantum (HCQ) Alzheimer's Classification via Supervised $β$-VAE and Quantum Kernels](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.14194)
*Tia Tiwari,Vamshi Krishna Kancharla,Neelam Sinha*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种两阶段混合经典-量子（HCQ）流水线，用于从3D T1加权结构MRI中进行二元阿尔茨海默病分类。通过3D β-VAE将MRI压缩为64维潜在编码，PLS选择6个最具区分性的成分并映射为旋转角度，编码到6量子比特寄存器中，利用量子核SVM进行分类。在ADNI-1数据集上，稳定性增强版达到72.1%准确率和0.799 AUC。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统方法在阿尔茨海默病MRI分类中面临高维特征提取和分类精度瓶颈，量子计算有望提升特征空间的表达能力。作者希望构建一个经典与量子互补的混合框架，使量子核直接作用于由监督自编码器端到端学习得到的疾病感知特征，而非预处理后的输入。

Method: 两阶段HCQ流水线：(1) 经典阶段：3D β-VAE在体素重建、KL散度和焦点分类损失下端到端训练，将3D MRI压缩为64维潜在编码；PLS选择6个最佳分离AD/CN的成分并缩放为旋转角度。(2) 量子阶段：使用ZZ量子特征映射将6个角度编码到6量子比特寄存器，计算N×N量子态重叠Gram矩阵，输入预计算核SVM进行分类。

Result: 在308例ADNI-1受试者（137例AD, 171例CN）上，基线模型准确率67.2%，AUC 0.759；稳定性增强变体准确率72.1%，AUC 0.799，交叉验证方差减半。3D Grad-CAM验证模型聚焦于与阿尔茨海默病相关的脑区。

Conclusion: HCQ混合流水线在AD分类任务中展现出性能提升和稳定性增强，可作为生物医学成像诊断分类的通用框架，适用于传统方法面临类似挑战的其他领域。

Abstract: This paper presents a two-stage Hybrid Classical-Quantum (HCQ) pipeline for binary Alzheimer's disease (AD) classification from 3D T1-weighted structural MRI volumes, where the classical and quantum components are designed to complement each other rather than operate independently. A supervised 3D $β$-variational autoencoder (VAE) is trained end-to-end under voxel-wise reconstruction, KL-divergence, and focal classification losses that compress each 3D MRI volume (resized from 152 x 184 x 152 to 96 x 96 x 96) into a 64-dimensional latent code. Partial Least Squares (PLS) regression selects the six components in the latent code that best separate Alzheimer's Disease (AD) from cognitively normal (CN) subjects and rescales them into rotation angles, which are encoded onto a six-qubit register using the ZZ quantum feature map to give us the respective quantum states. The input to a precomputed-kernel Support Vector Machine (SVM) is an N x N Gram matrix (N = 308), created by calculating the overlap between every pair of quantum states. The novelty of this work lies in the fact that the quantum kernel operates directly on disease-aware features that are learned end-to-end by a supervised autoencoder, rather than on pre-extracted inputs. On 308 ADNI-1 subjects, consisting of 137 AD and 171 CN subjects, the baseline achieved 67.2% accuracy and 0.759 AUC, while the stability-enhanced variant reached 72.1% accuracy and 0.799 AUC with cross-fold variance halved. 3D Grad-CAM further helped validate our model's focus on brain regions linked to Alzheimer's. The HCQ pipeline could serve as a general-purpose framework for diagnostic classification across biomedical imaging domains that present similar challenges for classical approaches.

</details>


### [190] [What Drives Test-Time Adaptation for CLIP? A Controlled Empirical Study from an Update Perspective](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.14299)
*Jiazhen Huang,Xiao Chen,Zhiming Liu,Yaru Sun,Jingyan Jiang,Zhi Wang*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 本文对CLIP模型的测试时自适应（TTA4CLIP）方法进行了系统性的控制实验研究，提出了统一的三大范式分类，构建了TTABC基准，揭示了参数自适应方法的驱动力主要来自测试时证据和可靠代理而非深度优化，证明了轻量级原型更新即可实现竞争性能，并指出没有一种适应范式能通用所有分布偏移场景。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有TTA4CLIP方法发展迅速，但缺乏对适应机制根本原理的理解——即什么真正驱动了适应、增益从何而来、在何种偏移下可靠。作者旨在填补这一认知空白。

Method: 1) 将现有方法分为三种统一范式（按测试时更新的内容划分）；2) 构建TTABC开源基准（标准化评估协议，集成20+代表性方法）；3) 从三个方面进行控制实验分析：参数方法的驱动因素、证据利用方式、不同偏移下范式的选择。

Result: 1) 参数方法的适应增益主要来自测试时证据和可靠代理，而非复杂优化；2) 通过跨样本/当前样本证据和轻量级原型更新即可实现竞争且高效的性能；3) 没有通用的最优适应范式，最优选择取决于偏移类型。

Conclusion: TTA4CLIP领域需要回归基本原理，理解不同适应机制的本质；TTABC基准和系统分析为后续研究提供了清晰的参考框架。

Abstract: Vision-Language Models (VLMs) such as CLIP have become a standard backbone for open-vocabulary recognition, yet their zero-shot predictions remain vulnerable to distribution shifts encountered at deployment. Test-Time Adaptation (TTA) has recently been extended to CLIP as a lightweight solution, leading to a rapidly growing body of TTA4CLIP methods. However, empirical progress in this area has largely outpaced our understanding of what truly drives adaptation, where their gains originate, and under which shifts they remain reliable. In this paper, we take a step back from the pursuit of state-of-the-art accuracy and conduct a systematic controlled study of TTA4CLIP. We first organize existing methods into three unified paradigms according to what is updated at test time. We then introduce TTABC, an open-source TTA Benchmark for CLIP, which standardizes evaluation protocols and integrates more than 20 representative methods. Our controlled empirical analysis focuses on three key areas. First, we determine the driving factors in parameter-based methods, revealing that adaptation gains are primarily driven by test-time evidence and reliable proxies rather than heavy optimization. Second, we explore evidence utilization beyond heavy parameter tuning, showing that competitive and efficient performance can be achieved through cross- or current-sample evidence and lightweight prototype updates. Finally, we demonstrate that there is no silver bullet for TTA: no single adaptation paradigm is universally optimal, and the preferred paradigm depends on the nature of shift. We hope our benchmark and study provide a clearer understanding of the current TTA4CLIP landscape and establish a foundation for further research.

</details>


### [191] [HumP-KD: A Hybrid Uncertainty-Aware Multi-Stage Progressive Knowledge Distillation Framework for Efficient Fire Classification](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.14684)
*Mohammed Arif Mainuddin,Najifa Tabassum,Omar Ibne Shahid,Riasat Khan*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 提出HumP-KD框架，通过层次化渐进知识蒸馏将两个异构Transformer教师的知识蒸馏到轻量MobileViT-S学生模型中，在火灾分类任务上达到高精度（F1=0.9876）的同时仅保留4.94M参数，适合实时部署。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 实时火灾分类系统需要同时满足高精度、计算高效和可在资源受限硬件上部署的要求，现有模型难以兼顾这些目标。

Method: 提出HumP-KD框架，包含三个紧密集成的组件：1）从两个冻结的异构Transformer教师（Swin-Tiny和ViT-Base）及其Meta-MLP集成中蒸馏知识；2）层次化渐进知识蒸馏（HPKD）使用层次化特征构建器生成融合空间注意力掩码，引导蒸馏聚焦于判别性区域；3）多阶段知识蒸馏（MSKD）在训练过程中逐步激活三个蒸馏阶段。

Result: 在Dataset-II上，HumP-KD达到0.9876±0.0063的F1分数，显著优于MobileViT-S基线（0.9537±0.0351），统计检验显著（p=0.0195, p=0.0039）。学生模型仅4.94M参数、19.01Mb大小，比Swin-Tiny减少5.7倍参数，比ViT-Base减少17.5倍，CPU推理达到37.72 FPS。

Conclusion: HumP-KD通过层次化多阶段知识蒸馏有效平衡了火灾分类任务的精度与效率，在多种退化条件下表现鲁棒，适合实时部署场景。

Abstract: Real-time fire classification systems require models that are simultaneously accurate, computationally efficient, and deployable on resource-constrained hardware. This work proposes \textbf{HumP-KD}, a Hybrid Uncertainty-aware Multi-stage Progressive Knowledge Distillation framework for efficient fire classification. Two datasets, FlameVision and Dataset-II, containing 8,600 and 31,309 images, are used. Various CNN and transformer baselines are applied under standard preprocessing, online augmentation, Gaussian noise and motion blur robustness conditions. The proposed HumP-KD model distills knowledge from two frozen heterogeneous transformer teachers, Swin-Tiny and ViT-Base, along with their Meta-MLP ensemble, into a lightweight MobileViT-S student via three tightly integrated components. Hierarchical Progressive Knowledge Distillation employs a Hierarchical Feature Builder. It generates a fused spatial attention mask to guide distillation toward discriminative regions selectively. Multi-Stage Knowledge Distillation progressively activates three distillation stages across training. On Dataset-II, HumP-KD achieves a mean F1 score of $0.9876 \pm 0.0063$ across 10 independent trials, significantly outperforming the MobileViT-S baseline trained without distillation ($0.9537 \pm 0.0351$), with statistical significance confirmed by both independent t-test ($p = 0.0195$) and Wilcoxon signed-rank test ($W = 1$, $p = 0.0039$). The proposed method also demonstrates strong generalization across datasets and robustness under degraded visual conditions. The student model retains only 4.94M parameters and 19.01Mb model size, representing a $5.7\times$ parameter reduction over Swin-Tiny and a $17.5\times$ reduction over ViT-Base, while achieving 37.72 CPU FPS, making it suitable for real-time deployment.

### [192] [Gaze Heads: How VLMs Look at What They Describe](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.14703)
*Rohit Gandikota,David Bau*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 本文发现VLM语言骨干中存在少量"凝视注意力头"(gaze heads)，其注意力跟踪当前描述的图像区域。通过干预这些头部（不超过9%），可以以83.1%的准确率将模型回答引导至任意选定的漫画面板，并扩展到自然图像控制和模型规模泛化。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: VLM内部如何解决图像描述任务尚不明确，作者希望通过机制分析揭示其内部运作，并找到无需重训练即可控制模型行为的实用方法。

Method: 1) 使用漫画条作为受控测试平台（叙事顺序空间排列）；2) 通过少量前向传播计算简单相关分数，发现凝视注意力头；3) 对这些头部进行注意力掩码干预，重定向模型注意力到指定区域；4) 扩展到连续控制（生成中切换凝视目标）和自然图像(COCO)验证。

Result: 1) 对前100个凝视头（<9%全部头）的单一干预，以83.1%准确率引导回答至任意漫画面板；2) 随机头部干预无效，干预所有头部破坏生成；3) 生成中切换凝视目标可在几个token内完成面板转换；4) 干预扩展到COCO自然图像有效；5) 机制在2B-32B参数规模和多种VLM架构中重现，但部分冻结编码器家族无此头部集。

Conclusion: 通过机制分析发现的目标编辑可以作为实用的推理时杠杆来引导多模态模型行为，无需任何重训练。这展示了可解释性研究对实际模型控制的直接价值。

Abstract: How a vision-language model internally solves the task of describing an image is far from obvious. We find that the model develops a specific mechanism for this: a small set of attention heads in its language-model backbone, which we call gaze heads, whose attention tracks the image region the model is currently describing. We find them with a simple correlation score from a few forward passes, using comic strips as a controlled testbed where narrative order is laid out spatially. These gaze heads do not just track the image tokens being described: redirecting their attention to a chosen region forces the VLM to describe that region instead. A single attention-mask intervention on the top-100 gaze heads, fewer than 9% of all heads, steers the model's answer to any chosen comic panel at 83.1% accuracy, while the same intervention on random heads fails to redirect the answer, and intervening on all heads destroys generation. The same lever also extends to continuous control: switching the gaze target mid-generation makes the model wrap up its current panel description and move to the new one within a few tokens. Beyond comics, the same intervention redirects answers to chosen regions in natural COCO images. The mechanism further recurs across model sizes from 2B to 32B parameters and across other VLM architectures, although some frozen-encoder families show no comparable head set. More broadly, this shows that targeted edits identified through mechanistic analysis can serve as practical inference-time levers for steering multimodal model behavior, without any retraining. Our code, interactive demo, and datasets are available at https://gaze.baulab.info/

</details>


<div id='math.CO'></div>

# math.CO [[Back]](#toc)

### [193] [Biclique decompositions from Welzl orders](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.09785)
*Jean Cardinal,Rose McCarty,Yelena Yuditsky*

Main category: math.CO

TL;DR: 本文研究了可通过双团分解紧凑表示的图类（顶点邻域为子线性个区间的并集），并利用Welzl（1988）的低邻域复杂度图排序结果，恢复并扩展了Zarankiewicz问题、矩阵乘法、量子电路复杂度和最短路径算法等多个已知结果（误差在对数因子内）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 为具有低邻域复杂度的图类寻找紧凑的双团分解表示，并以此统一证明多个不同领域（极值图论、算法、计算复杂性）的已知上界。

Method: 1. 证明若图的顶点可排序使得每个顶点的邻域是子线性个区间的并集，则该图存在小尺寸的双团分解（尺寸为各双团的顶点数之和）。2. 利用Welzl（1988）的低邻域复杂度图类存在此类排序的结论，将双团分解结果应用于具体问题。

Result: 恢复并扩展了以下结果的对数因子版本：(1) Zarankiewicz问题的上界；(2) 矩阵乘法的复杂度界；(3) 量子电路复杂度的上界；(4) "结构良好"实例中最短路径算法的上界。

Conclusion: 双团分解是连接图邻域复杂性与多个计算问题复杂度上界的统一工具，且该框架能系统性地改进或恢复已有结论。

Abstract: A biclique decomposition of a graph is a partition of its edges into complete bipartite subgraphs. We consider graphs whose vertices can be ordered such that the neighborhood of every vertex is the union of a sublinear number of intervals. We observe that these graphs admit compact representations in the form of biclique decompositions of small size. Here, the size of a decomposition is measured as the sum of the number of vertices of its bicliques. Combining this result with the existence of suitable vertex orderings for graphs of low neighborhood complexity, as proven by Welzl in 1988, we recover and extend several known results up to logarithmic factors. These results include upper bounds on the Zarankiewicz problem, matrix multiplication, quantum circuit complexity, and shortest path algorithms in ``well-structured'' instances.

</details>
